    "body": "Yes, I'm changing that pattern in 4.0. Each database has it's own sub-module now so it is even enforced by the compiler. I haven't pushed the 4.0 branch for a while because it's very torn apart, but I think it is significantly improved by removing all \"database instanceof \" logic out of liquibase-core. \n\nI was able to handle most of the isAfterColumnClauseOk() style logic by allowing database-specific logic to more easily reorder SQL clauses, introducing some Database-level methods like \"requiresExplicitNullDefinitions\", and  a more general AlterColumnAction that handle database-specific differences like \"ALTER COLUMN\"  vs \"MODIFY COLUMN\"\n",

    "created_at": "2019-01-08T08:51:45Z",
    "updated_at": "2019-01-08T08:51:45Z",
    "author_association": "MEMBER",
    "body": "Here is a scetch for some testing of mocking modularized types:\r\n\r\n```java\r\nimport static net.bytebuddy.matcher.ElementMatchers.named;\r\n\r\nimport java.io.IOException;\r\nimport java.lang.module.Configuration;\r\nimport java.lang.module.ModuleFinder;\r\nimport java.nio.file.Files;\r\nimport java.nio.file.Path;\r\nimport java.util.Collections;\r\nimport java.util.concurrent.Callable;\r\nimport java.util.jar.JarEntry;\r\nimport java.util.jar.JarOutputStream;\r\n\r\nimport org.mockito.Mockito;\r\n\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.ByteBuddy;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.description.modifier.Visibility;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.implementation.FixedValue;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.jar.asm.ClassWriter;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.jar.asm.ModuleVisitor;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.jar.asm.Opcodes;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.utility.OpenedClassReader;\r\n\r\npublic class MyTest {\r\n\r\n    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {\r\n        Path jar = modularJar(true, true, true);\r\n        ModuleLayer layer = layer(jar);\r\n\r\n        Class<?> type = layer.findLoader(\"mockito.test\").loadClass(\"sample.MyCallable\");\r\n        @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\r\n        Callable<String> mock = (Callable<String>) Mockito.mock(type);\r\n        Mockito.when(mock.call()).thenCallRealMethod();\r\n        Object result = mock.call();\r\n\r\n        // We should have a check that fails mock creation of mock cannot be loaded in target class loader.\r\n        \r\n        System.out.println(mock.getClass().getName()); // org.mockito.codegen only if opened = false\r\n        System.out.println(result); // should be 'foo'\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    private static Path modularJar(boolean publik, boolean exported, boolean opened) throws IOException {\r\n        Path jar = Files.createTempFile(\"sample-module\", \".jar\");\r\n        try (JarOutputStream out = new JarOutputStream(Files.newOutputStream(jar))) {\r\n            out.putNextEntry(new JarEntry(\"module-info.class\"));\r\n            out.write(moduleInfo(exported, opened));\r\n            out.closeEntry();\r\n            out.putNextEntry(new JarEntry(\"sample/MyCallable.class\"));\r\n            out.write(type(publik));\r\n            out.closeEntry();\r\n        }\r\n        return jar;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    private static byte[] type(boolean publik) {\r\n        return new ByteBuddy()\r\n            .subclass(Callable.class)\r\n            .name(\"sample.MyCallable\")\r\n            .merge(publik ? Visibility.PUBLIC : Visibility.PACKAGE_PRIVATE)\r\n            .method(named(\"call\"))\r\n            .intercept(FixedValue.value(\"foo\"))\r\n            .make()\r\n            .getBytes();\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    private static byte[] moduleInfo(boolean exported, boolean opened) {\r\n        ClassWriter classWriter = new ClassWriter(OpenedClassReader.ASM_API);\r\n        classWriter.visit(Opcodes.V9, Opcodes.ACC_MODULE, \"module-info\", null, null, null);\r\n        ModuleVisitor mv = classWriter.visitModule(\"mockito.test\", 0, null);\r\n        mv.visitRequire(\"java.base\", Opcodes.ACC_MANDATED, null);\r\n        mv.visitPackage(\"sample\");\r\n        if (exported) {\r\n            mv.visitExport(\"sample\", 0);\r\n        }\r\n        if (opened) {\r\n            mv.visitOpen(\"sample\", 0);\r\n        }\r\n        mv.visitEnd();\r\n        classWriter.visitEnd();\r\n        return classWriter.toByteArray();\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    private static ModuleLayer layer(Path jar) {\r\n        Configuration configuration = Configuration.resolve(\r\n            ModuleFinder.of(jar),\r\n            Collections.singletonList(ModuleLayer.boot().configuration()),\r\n            ModuleFinder.of(),\r\n            Collections.singleton(\"mockito.test\")\r\n        );\r\n\r\n        return ModuleLayer.defineModulesWithOneLoader(\r\n            configuration,\r\n            Collections.singletonList(ModuleLayer.boot()),\r\n            null\r\n        ).layer();\r\n    }\r\n}\r\n```\r\n\r\n@TimvdLippe Could you integrate a test using Java 9 into the build somehow? If you achieve that, I would add some more logic that I think we should integrate for better error messages.",

    "updated_at": "2019-01-08T08:51:45Z",
    "author_association": "MEMBER",
    "body": "Here is a scetch for some testing of mocking modularized types:\r\n\r\n```java\r\nimport static net.bytebuddy.matcher.ElementMatchers.named;\r\n\r\nimport java.io.IOException;\r\nimport java.lang.module.Configuration;\r\nimport java.lang.module.ModuleFinder;\r\nimport java.nio.file.Files;\r\nimport java.nio.file.Path;\r\nimport java.util.Collections;\r\nimport java.util.concurrent.Callable;\r\nimport java.util.jar.JarEntry;\r\nimport java.util.jar.JarOutputStream;\r\n\r\nimport org.mockito.Mockito;\r\n\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.ByteBuddy;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.description.modifier.Visibility;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.implementation.FixedValue;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.jar.asm.ClassWriter;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.jar.asm.ModuleVisitor;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.jar.asm.Opcodes;\r\nimport net.bytebuddy.utility.OpenedClassReader;\r\n\r\npublic class MyTest {\r\n\r\n    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {\r\n        Path jar = modularJar(true, true, true);\r\n        ModuleLayer layer = layer(jar);\r\n\r\n        Class<?> type = layer.findLoader(\"mockito.test\").loadClass(\"sample.MyCallable\");\r\n        @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\r\n        Callable<String> mock = (Callable<String>) Mockito.mock(type);\r\n        Mockito.when(mock.call()).thenCallRealMethod();\r\n        Object result = mock.call();\r\n\r\n        // We should have a check that fails mock creation of mock cannot be loaded in target class loader.\r\n        \r\n        System.out.println(mock.getClass().getName()); // org.mockito.codegen only if opened = false\r\n        System.out.println(result); // should be 'foo'\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    private static Path modularJar(boolean publik, boolean exported, boolean opened) throws IOException {\r\n        Path jar = Files.createTempFile(\"sample-module\", \".jar\");\r\n        try (JarOutputStream out = new JarOutputStream(Files.newOutputStream(jar))) {\r\n            out.putNextEntry(new JarEntry(\"module-info.class\"));\r\n            out.write(moduleInfo(exported, opened));\r\n            out.closeEntry();\r\n            out.putNextEntry(new JarEntry(\"sample/MyCallable.class\"));\r\n            out.write(type(publik));\r\n            out.closeEntry();\r\n        }\r\n        return jar;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    private static byte[] type(boolean publik) {\r\n        return new ByteBuddy()\r\n            .subclass(Callable.class)\r\n            .name(\"sample.MyCallable\")\r\n            .merge(publik ? Visibility.PUBLIC : Visibility.PACKAGE_PRIVATE)\r\n            .method(named(\"call\"))\r\n            .intercept(FixedValue.value(\"foo\"))\r\n            .make()\r\n            .getBytes();\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    private static byte[] moduleInfo(boolean exported, boolean opened) {\r\n        ClassWriter classWriter = new ClassWriter(OpenedClassReader.ASM_API);\r\n        classWriter.visit(Opcodes.V9, Opcodes.ACC_MODULE, \"module-info\", null, null, null);\r\n        ModuleVisitor mv = classWriter.visitModule(\"mockito.test\", 0, null);\r\n        mv.visitRequire(\"java.base\", Opcodes.ACC_MANDATED, null);\r\n        mv.visitPackage(\"sample\");\r\n        if (exported) {\r\n            mv.visitExport(\"sample\", 0);\r\n        }\r\n        if (opened) {\r\n            mv.visitOpen(\"sample\", 0);\r\n        }\r\n        mv.visitEnd();\r\n        classWriter.visitEnd();\r\n        return classWriter.toByteArray();\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    private static ModuleLayer layer(Path jar) {\r\n        Configuration configuration = Configuration.resolve(\r\n            ModuleFinder.of(jar),\r\n            Collections.singletonList(ModuleLayer.boot().configuration()),\r\n            ModuleFinder.of(),\r\n            Collections.singleton(\"mockito.test\")\r\n        );\r\n\r\n        return ModuleLayer.defineModulesWithOneLoader(\r\n            configuration,\r\n            Collections.singletonList(ModuleLayer.boot()),\r\n            null\r\n        ).layer();\r\n    }\r\n}\r\n```\r\n\r\n@TimvdLippe Could you integrate a test using Java 9 into the build somehow? If you achieve that, I would add some more logic that I think we should integrate for better error messages.",
